\subsection{Detailed Description}
Apache Kafka C/\-C++ consumer and producer client library. \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h}{rdkafka.\-h} contains the public A\-P\-I for librdkafka. The A\-P\-I is documented in this file as comments prefixing the function, type, enum, define, etc.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
For the C++ interface see 

\hyperlink{rdkafkacpp_8h_source}{rdkafkacpp.\-h} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Supported debug contexts. (compile time) 

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000001}{Deprecated}]This compile time value may be outdated at runtime due to linking another version of the library. Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_adece97d3cbdd6ca936df5b0663118c45}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-get\-\_\-debug\-\_\-contexts()} instead. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a21be13f8a4cb1d5aff01419f333e5ea7}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E@{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E}}
\index{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E@{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E~0x1  /$\ast$ Delegate freeing of payload to rdkafka. $\ast$/}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a21be13f8a4cb1d5aff01419f333e5ea7}
Produce and send a single message to broker.

'rkt' is the target topic which must have been previously created with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-new()}}.

{\ttfamily rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-produce()} is an asynch non-\/blocking A\-P\-I.

'partition' is the target partition, either\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-P\-A\-R\-T\-I\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-U\-A (unassigned) for automatic partitioning using the topic's partitioner function, or
\item a fixed partition (0..N)
\end{DoxyItemize}

'msgflags' is zero or more of the following flags O\-R\-:ed together\-: R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E -\/ rdkafka will free(3) 'payload' when it is done with it. R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-C\-O\-P\-Y -\/ the 'payload' data will be copied and the 'payload' pointer will not be used by rdkafka after the call returns.

..\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E and ..\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-C\-O\-P\-Y are mutually exclusive.

If the function returns -\/1 and R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-F\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E was specified, then the memory associated with the payload is still the caller's responsibility.

'payload' is the message payload of size 'len' bytes.

'key' is an optional message key of size 'keylen' bytes, if non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L it will be passed to the topic partitioner as well as be sent with the message to the broker and passed on to the consumer.

'msg\-\_\-opaque' is an optional application-\/provided per-\/message opaque pointer that will provided in the delivery report callback ({\ttfamily dr\-\_\-cb}) for referencing this message.

Returns 0 on success or -\/1 on error in which case errno is set accordingly\-: E\-N\-O\-B\-U\-F\-S -\/ maximum number of outstanding messages has been reached\-: \char`\"{}queue.\-buffering.\-max.\-messages\char`\"{} (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-Q\-U\-E\-U\-E\-\_\-\-F\-U\-L\-L) E\-M\-S\-G\-S\-I\-Z\-E -\/ message is larger than configured max size\-: \char`\"{}messages.\-max.\-bytes\char`\"{}. (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-M\-S\-G\-\_\-\-S\-I\-Z\-E\-\_\-\-T\-O\-O\-\_\-\-L\-A\-R\-G\-E) E\-S\-R\-C\-H -\/ requested 'partition' is unknown in the Kafka cluster. (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-\-P\-A\-R\-T\-I\-T\-I\-O\-N) E\-N\-O\-E\-N\-T -\/ topic is unknown in the Kafka cluster. (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-\-T\-O\-P\-I\-C)

N\-O\-T\-E\-: Use {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a99c7d1faaa534befeedf23b55a88a40f}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-errno2err()}} to convert {\ttfamily errno} to rdkafka error code. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a32dc6dd93c16e3aac9b89804c4817fba}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-B\-E\-G\-I\-N\-N\-I\-N\-G@{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-B\-E\-G\-I\-N\-N\-I\-N\-G}}
\index{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-B\-E\-G\-I\-N\-N\-I\-N\-G@{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-B\-E\-G\-I\-N\-N\-I\-N\-G}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}

Unassigned partition. 

The unassigned partition is used by the producer A\-P\-I for messages that should be partitioned using the configured or default partitioner. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa2e242fb8620a32b650a40575bc7f98e}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N@{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N}}
\index{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N@{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N~0x000900ff}}\label{rdkafka_8h_aa2e242fb8620a32b650a40575bc7f98e}


librdkafka version 

Interpreted as hex {\ttfamily M\-M.\-mm.\-rr.\-xx}\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item M\-M = Major
\item mm = minor
\item rr = revision
\item xx = pre-\/release id (0xff is the final release)
\end{DoxyItemize}

E.\-g.\-: {\ttfamily 0x000801ff} = 0.\-8.\-1

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This value should only be used during compile time, for runtime checks of version use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a83e363606ef2da2e91b7429b229dbc8e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-version()} 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a03509bab51072c72a8dcf52337e6d5cb}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t}}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a03509bab51072c72a8dcf52337e6d5cb}


Error codes. 

The negative error codes delimited by two underscores ({\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-}..) denotes errors internal to librdkafka and are displayed as {\ttfamily "Local\-:} $<$error string..$>$", while the error codes delimited by a single underscore ({\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-}..) denote broker errors and are displayed as {\ttfamily "Broker\-:} $<$error string..$>$".

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab7bfc925e8d63851511b88a1cee94d6d}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-err2str()} to translate an error code a human readable string 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab83da8da989fe41693d78d982c7ae6b7}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-brokers\-\_\-add@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-brokers\-\_\-add}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-brokers\-\_\-add@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-brokers\-\_\-add}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-brokers\-\_\-add}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-brokers\-\_\-add (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rk, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{brokerlist}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_ab83da8da989fe41693d78d982c7ae6b7}
Adds one or more brokers to the kafka handle's list of initial brokers. Additional brokers will be discovered automatically as soon as rdkafka connects to a broker by querying the broker metadata.

If a broker name resolves to multiple addresses (and possibly address families) all will be used for connection attempts in round-\/robin fashion.

'brokerlist' is a ,-\/separated list of brokers in the format\-: $<$broker1$>$,$<$broker2$>$,.. Where each broker is in either the host or U\-R\-L based format\-: $<$host$>$\mbox{[}\-:$<$port$>$\mbox{]} $<$proto$>$\-://$<$host$>$\mbox{[}\-:port\mbox{]} $<$proto$>$ is either P\-L\-A\-I\-N\-T\-E\-X\-T or S\-S\-L. The two formats can be mixed but ultimately the value of the {\ttfamily security.\-protocol} config property decides what brokers are allowed.

Example\-: brokerlist = \char`\"{}broker1\-:10000,broker2\char`\"{} brokerlist = \char`\"{}\-S\-S\-L\-://broker3\-:9000,broker1\-:10000,ssl\-://broker2\char`\"{}

Returns the number of brokers successfully added.

N\-O\-T\-E\-: Brokers may also be defined with the 'metadata.\-broker.\-list' configuration property. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a6eba851c2af748de6921d708b47dc94c}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T const char$\ast$$\ast$ rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{cntp}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a6eba851c2af748de6921d708b47dc94c}
Dump the configuration properties and values of {\ttfamily conf} to an array with \char`\"{}key\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}value\char`\"{} pairs. The number of entries in the array is returned in {\ttfamily $\ast$cntp}.

The dump must be freed with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8fee1254096acd17cbd61cfe70d827e5}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free()}}. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8fee1254096acd17cbd61cfe70d827e5}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump\-\_\-free (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$$\ast$}]{arr, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{cnt}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a8fee1254096acd17cbd61cfe70d827e5}
Frees a configuration dump returned from {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a6eba851c2af748de6921d708b47dc94c}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump()}} or `rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dump(). \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dup@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dup}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dup@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dup}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dup}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t$\ast$ rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dup (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{conf}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}
Creates a copy/duplicate of configuration object 'conf'. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_abe9f0f77e9145eb1a62c3258ac495b97}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-get@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-get}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-get@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-get}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-res\-\_\-t} rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-get (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name, }
\item[{char $\ast$}]{dest, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{dest\-\_\-size}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_abe9f0f77e9145eb1a62c3258ac495b97}
Retrieve configuration value for property {\ttfamily name}.

If {\ttfamily dest} is non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L the value will be written to {\ttfamily dest} with at most {\ttfamily dest\-\_\-size}.

{\ttfamily $\ast$dest\-\_\-size} is updated to the full length of the value, thus if {\ttfamily $\ast$dest\-\_\-size} initially is smaller than the full length the application may reallocate {\ttfamily dest} to fit the returned {\ttfamily $\ast$dest\-\_\-size} and try again.

If {\ttfamily dest} is N\-U\-L\-L only the full length of the value is returned.

Returns R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-F\-\_\-\-O\-K if the property name matched, else R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-F\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa7459bd22e8cfa81aa8c2480a4a0304c}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t$\ast$ rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_aa7459bd22e8cfa81aa8c2480a4a0304c}


Create configuration object. 

When providing your own configuration to the {\ttfamily rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-$\ast$\-\_\-new\-\_\-$\ast$}() calls the rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t objects needs to be created with this function which will set up the defaults. I.\-e.\-: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
*   rd\_kafka\_conf\_t *myconf;
*   \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad8306a08e59e8e2cbc6abdb84f9689f4}{rd\_kafka\_conf\_res\_t} res;
*
*   myconf = \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa7459bd22e8cfa81aa8c2480a4a0304c}{rd\_kafka\_conf\_new}();
*   res = \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_abb1b319278333e8cdee9442da7f135e8}{rd\_kafka\_conf\_set}(myconf, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"socket.timeout.ms"}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"600"},
*                           errstr, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(errstr));
*   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (res != \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad8306a08e59e8e2cbc6abdb84f9689f4a12343fa082ab52164a17130d6b0d0f5b}{RD\_KAFKA\_CONF\_OK})
*      die(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"%s\(\backslash\)n"}, errstr);
*   
*   rk = \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\_kafka\_new}(..., myconf);
* 
\end{DoxyCode}


Please see C\-O\-N\-F\-I\-G\-U\-R\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N.\-md for the default settings or use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa52f3a5a08207e14386739fe336e57be}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-properties\-\_\-show()} to provide the information at runtime.

The properties are identical to the Apache Kafka configuration properties whenever possible.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t object with defaults set.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_abb1b319278333e8cdee9442da7f135e8}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_af3669dacf78c5c0eb536d65cb45d0491}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-destroy()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

In case of failure 'errstr' is updated to contain a human readable error string. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a65eaf45e9b26bcb085f4651634ce06a5}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-consume\-\_\-cb@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-consume\-\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-consume\-\_\-cb@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-consume\-\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}

Consumer\-: Set consume callback for use with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-poll()}}. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a138aa4881c8703dd6b69f22ddc454f63}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-default\-\_\-topic\-\_\-conf@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-default\-\_\-topic\-\_\-conf}}

Consumer\-: Set rebalance callback for use with coordinated consumer group balancing. Set socket callback. The socket callback is responsible for opening a socket according to the supplied domain, type and protocol. The socket shall be created with C\-L\-O\-E\-X\-E\-C set in a racefree fashion, if possible.

Default\-: on linux\-: racefree C\-L\-O\-E\-X\-E\-C others \-: non-\/racefree C\-L\-O\-E\-X\-E\-C \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a597d00432e3ca22174d18e7e348fb766}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-stats\-\_\-cb@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-stats\-\_\-cb}}

\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{conf, }

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a597d00432e3ca22174d18e7e348fb766}
Set statistics callback in provided conf object. The statistics callback is called from {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll()}} every {\ttfamily statistics.\-interval.\-ms} (needs to be configured separately). Function arguments\-: 'rk' -\/ Kafka handle 'json' -\/ String containing the statistics data in J\-S\-O\-N format 'json\-\_\-len' -\/ Length of 'json' string. 'opaque' -\/ Application-\/provided opaque.

If the application wishes to hold on to the 'json' pointer and free it at a later time it must return 1 from the {\ttfamily stats\-\_\-cb}. If the application returns 0 from the {\ttfamily stats\-\_\-cb} then librdkafka will immediately free the 'json' pointer. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a04160826ad039d42c10edec456163fa7}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-throttle\-\_\-cb@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-throttle\-\_\-cb}}

\item[{void($\ast$)(rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t $\ast$rk, const char $\ast$broker\-\_\-name, int32\-\_\-t broker\-\_\-id, int throttle\-\_\-time\-\_\-ms, void $\ast$opaque)}]{throttle\-\_\-cb}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a04160826ad039d42c10edec456163fa7}
Set throttle callback. The throttle callback is used in conjunction with {\ttfamily quota.\-support.\-enable=true} to forward broker throttle times for Produce and Fetch (consume) requests.

Callbacks are called whenever a non-\/zero throttle time is returned by the broker, or when the throttle time drops back to zero. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t}$\ast$ rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition, }
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}
Consume a single message from topic 'rkt' and 'partition'.

'timeout\-\_\-ms' is maximum amount of time to wait for a message to be received. Consumer must have been previously started with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start()}}.

Returns a message object on success and N\-U\-L\-L on error. The message object must be destroyed with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a35e0c519209d1afe9e29468f766c1c24}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-destroy()}} when the application is done with it.

Errors (when returning N\-U\-L\-L)\-: E\-T\-I\-M\-E\-D\-O\-U\-T -\/ 'timeout\-\_\-ms' was reached with no new messages fetched. E\-N\-O\-E\-N\-T -\/ 'rkt'+'partition' is unknown. (no prior {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start()}} call)

N\-O\-T\-E\-: The returned message's '..-\/$>$err' must be checked for errors. N\-O\-T\-E\-: '..-\/$>$err == R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-P\-A\-R\-T\-I\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-E\-O\-F' signals that the end of the partition has been reached, which should typically not be considered an error. The application should handle this case (e.\-g., ignore). \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T ssize\-\_\-t rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition, }
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms, }
\item[{{\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$}]{rkmessages, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{rkmessages\-\_\-size}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}
Consume up to 'rkmessages\-\_\-size' from topic 'rkt' and 'partition', putting a pointer to each message in the application provided array 'rkmessages' (of size 'rkmessages\-\_\-size' entries).

{\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch()}} provides higher throughput performance than {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume()}}.

'timeout\-\_\-ms' is the maximum amount of time to wait for all of 'rkmessages\-\_\-size' messages to be put into 'rkmessages'. If no messages were available within the timeout period this function returns 0 and {\ttfamily rkmessages} remains untouched. This differs somewhat from {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume()}}.

The message objects must be destroyed with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a35e0c519209d1afe9e29468f766c1c24}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-destroy()}} when the application is done with it.

Returns the number of rkmessages added in 'rkmessages', or -\/1 on error (same error codes as for {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume()}}.

See\-: rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a3d949238471993b18537855aad28fa23}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch\-\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch\-\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch\-\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T ssize\-\_\-t rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch\-\_\-queue (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkqu, }
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms, }
\item[{{\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$}]{rkmessages, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{rkmessages\-\_\-size}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a3d949238471993b18537855aad28fa23}
See {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch()}} above. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition, }
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms, }
\item[{void($\ast$)({\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$opaque)}]{consume\-\_\-cb, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{opaque}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}
Consumes messages from topic 'rkt' and 'partition', calling the provided callback for each consumed messsage.

{\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback()}} provides higher throughput performance than both {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume()}} and {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-batch()}}.

'timeout\-\_\-ms' is the maximum amount of time to wait for one or more messages to arrive.

The provided 'consume\-\_\-cb' function is called for each message, the application must N\-O\-T call {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a35e0c519209d1afe9e29468f766c1c24}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-destroy()}} on the provided 'rkmessage'.

The 'opaque' argument is passed to the 'consume\-\_\-cb' as 'opaque'.

Returns the number of messages processed or -\/1 on error.

See\-: rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_abb1aaca2499c2e7d6da37dc28953d532}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback\-\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback\-\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback\-\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback\-\_\-queue (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkqu, }
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms, }
\item[{void($\ast$)({\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$opaque)}]{consume\-\_\-cb, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{opaque}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_abb1aaca2499c2e7d6da37dc28953d532}
See {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback()}} above. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t}$\ast$ rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkqu, }
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}
Queue consumers

The following {\ttfamily ...\-\_\-queue()} functions are analogue to the functions above but reads messages from the provided queue {\ttfamily rkqu} instead. {\ttfamily rkqu} must have been previously created with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a2b59178eb7e88d40510a89f3f2d98b44}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-new()}} and the topic consumer must have been started with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue()}} utilising the the same queue. See {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume()}} above. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition, }
\item[{int64\-\_\-t}]{offset}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}
Start consuming messages for topic 'rkt' and 'partition' at offset 'offset' which may either be an absolute (0..N) or one of the logical offsets\-: {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-B\-E\-G\-I\-N\-N\-I\-N\-G}, {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-E\-N\-D}, {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-S\-T\-O\-R\-E\-D}, {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-O\-F\-F\-S\-E\-T\-\_\-\-T\-A\-I\-L(..)}

rdkafka will attempt to keep 'queued.\-min.\-messages' (config property) messages in the local queue by repeatedly fetching batches of messages from the broker until the threshold is reached.

The application shall use one of the {\ttfamily rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume$\ast$()} functions to consume messages from the local queue, each kafka message being represented as a {\ttfamily \hyperlink{structrd__kafka__message__t}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-message\-\_\-t} $\ast$} object.

{\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start()}} must not be called multiple times for the same topic and partition without stopping consumption first with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop()}}.

Returns 0 on success or -\/1 on error in which case errno is set accordingly\-: E\-B\-U\-S\-Y -\/ Conflicts with an existing or previous subscription (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-F\-L\-I\-C\-T) E\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L -\/ Invalid offset, or incomplete configuration (lacking group.\-id) (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-\_\-\-A\-R\-G) E\-S\-R\-C\-H -\/ requested 'partition' is invalid. (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-\-P\-A\-R\-T\-I\-T\-I\-O\-N) E\-N\-O\-E\-N\-T -\/ topic is unknown in the Kafka cluster. (R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-U\-N\-K\-N\-O\-W\-N\-\_\-\-T\-O\-P\-I\-C)

Use {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a99c7d1faaa534befeedf23b55a88a40f}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-errno2err()}} to convert {\ttfamily errno} to {\ttfamily rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t}. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition, }
\item[{int64\-\_\-t}]{offset, }
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkqu}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}
Same as \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start()} but re-\/routes incoming messages to the provided queue 'rkqu' (which must have been previously allocated with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a2b59178eb7e88d40510a89f3f2d98b44}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-new()}}. The application must use one of the {\ttfamily rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-$\ast$\-\_\-queue()} functions to receive fetched messages.

{\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue()}} must not be called multiple times for the same topic and partition without stopping consumption first with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop()}}. {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start()}} and {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue()}} must not be combined for the same topic and partition. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-stop (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}
Stop consuming messages for topic 'rkt' and 'partition', purging all messages currently in the local queue.

N\-O\-T\-E\-: To enforce synchronisation this call will block until the internal fetcher has terminated and offsets are commited to configured storage method.

The application needs to be stop all consumers before calling {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-destroy()}} on the main object handle.

Returns 0 on success or -\/1 on error (see {\ttfamily errno}). \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a37b54d329e12d745889defe96e7d043d}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-close@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-close}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-close@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-close}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-close}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t} rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consumer\-\_\-close (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rk}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a37b54d329e12d745889defe96e7d043d}


Close down the Kafka\-Consumer. 

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This call will block until the consumer has revoked its assignment, calling the {\ttfamily rebalance\-\_\-cb} if it is configured, committed offsets to broker, and left the consumer group.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An error code indicating if the consumer close was succesful or not.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The application still needs to call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-destroy()} after this call finishes to clean up the underlying handle resources. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

Returns this client's broker-\/assigned group member id. 

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This currently requires the high-\/level Kafka\-Consumer
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An allocated string containing the current broker-\/assigned group member id, or N\-U\-L\-L if not available. The application must free the string with {\ttfamily free()} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{conf, }

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}
Creates a new Kafka handle and starts its operation according to the specified {\ttfamily type} ({\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-S\-U\-M\-E\-R} or {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-P\-R\-O\-D\-U\-C\-E\-R}).

{\ttfamily conf} is an optional struct created with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa7459bd22e8cfa81aa8c2480a4a0304c}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new()}} that will be used instead of the default configuration. The {\ttfamily conf} object is freed by this function and must not be used or destroyed by the application sub-\/sequently. See {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_abb1b319278333e8cdee9442da7f135e8}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set()}} et.\-al for more information.

{\ttfamily errstr} must be a pointer to memory of at least size {\ttfamily errstr\-\_\-size} where {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-new()}} may write a human readable error message in case the creation of a new handle fails. In which case the function returns N\-U\-L\-L.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
{\bfseries R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-S\-U\-M\-E\-R\-:} When a new {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-S\-U\-M\-E\-R} rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t handle is created it may either operate in the legacy simple consumer mode using the \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start()} interface, or the High-\/level Kafka\-Consumer A\-P\-I. 

An application must only use one of these groups of A\-P\-Is on a given rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-S\-U\-M\-E\-R handle.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The Kafka handle on success or N\-U\-L\-L on error (see {\ttfamily errstr})
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
To destroy the Kafka handle, use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-destroy()}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Topic+partition offset store.

If auto.\-commit.\-enable is true the offset is stored automatically prior to returning of the message(s) in each of the rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume$\ast$() functions above. Store offset 'offset' for topic 'rkt' partition 'partition'. The offset will be commited (written) to the offset store according to {\ttfamily auto.\-commit.\-interval.\-ms}.

N\-O\-T\-E\-: {\ttfamily auto.\-commit.\-enable} must be set to \char`\"{}false\char`\"{} when using this A\-P\-I.

Returns R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-O\-R on success or an error code on error. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_af006d797a3db9c80d9bc08b2d4af93da}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-opaque@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-opaque}}

Returns the current out queue length\-: messages waiting to be sent to, or acknowledged by, the broker. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll}}

\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}
Polls the provided kafka handle for events.

Events will cause application provided callbacks to be called.

The 'timeout\-\_\-ms' argument specifies the minimum amount of time (in milliseconds) that the call will block waiting for events. For non-\/blocking calls, provide 0 as 'timeout\-\_\-ms'. To wait indefinately for an event, provide -\/1.

Events\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item delivery report callbacks (if dr\-\_\-cb is configured) \mbox{[}producer\mbox{]}
\item error callbacks (if error\-\_\-cb is configured) \mbox{[}producer \& consumer\mbox{]}
\item stats callbacks (if stats\-\_\-cb is configured) \mbox{[}producer \& consumer\mbox{]}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns the number of events served. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a9bfa0a1dd3f866cbf0c82fc089bd7904}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll\-\_\-set\-\_\-consumer@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll\-\_\-set\-\_\-consumer}}

Experimental A\-P\-Is. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a7ad15c71f228c47946500a0e5c6f88ed}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-produce\-\_\-batch@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-produce\-\_\-batch}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a7ad15c71f228c47946500a0e5c6f88ed}
Produce multiple messages.

If partition is R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-P\-A\-R\-T\-I\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-U\-A the configured partitioner will be run for each message (slower), otherwise the messages will be enqueued to the specified partition directly (faster).

The messages are provided in the array {\ttfamily rkmessages} of count {\ttfamily message\-\_\-cnt} elements. The {\ttfamily partition} and {\ttfamily msgflags} are used for all provided messages.

Honoured {\ttfamily rkmessages\mbox{[}\mbox{]}} fields are\-: payload,len -\/ Message payload and length key,key\-\_\-len -\/ Optional message key \-\_\-private -\/ Message opaque pointer (msg\-\_\-opaque) err -\/ Will be set according to success or failure. Application only needs to check for errors if return value != {\ttfamily message\-\_\-cnt}.

Returns the number of messages succesfully enqueued for producing. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-destroy@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-queue\-\_\-destroy}}

Create a new message queue. 

See \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-start\-\_\-queue()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-queue()}, et.\-al. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a6667b162931982e9827e3d86ad22ec7d}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-seek@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-seek}}

\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-seek}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t} rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-seek (

)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a6667b162931982e9827e3d86ad22ec7d}
Seek consumer for topic+partition to {\ttfamily offset} which is either an absolute or logical offset.

If {\ttfamily timeout\-\_\-ms} is not 0 the call will wait this long for the seek to be performed. If the timeout is reached the internal state will be unknown and this function returns {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-T\-I\-M\-E\-D\-\_\-\-O\-U\-T}. If {\ttfamily timeout\-\_\-ms} is 0 it will initiate the seek but return immediately without any error reporting.

This call triggers a fetch queue barrier flush.

Returns {\ttfamily R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-R\-E\-S\-P\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-O\-R} on success else an error code. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acadeefced6bb60acd27e7a0dad553aa4}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-set\-\_\-log\-\_\-level@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-set\-\_\-log\-\_\-level}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Set logger function. The default is to print to stderr, but a syslog logger is also available, see rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-log\-\_\-(print$|$syslog) for the builtin alternatives. Alternatively the application may provide its own logger callback. Or pass 'func' as N\-U\-L\-L to disable logging.

D\-E\-P\-R\-E\-C\-A\-T\-E\-D, use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a06ade2ca41f32eb82c6f7e3d4acbe19f}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set\-\_\-log\-\_\-cb()}

N\-O\-T\-E\-: 'rk' may be passed as N\-U\-L\-L in the callback. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a0ebe15e9d0f39ccc84e9686f0fcf46f1}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-subscribe@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-subscribe}}

Subscribe to topic set using balanced consumer groups. 

Wildcard (regex) topics are supported by the librdkafka assignor\-: any topic name in the {\ttfamily topics} list that is prefixed with {\ttfamily "$^\wedge$"} will be regex-\/matched to the full list of topics in the cluster and matching topics will be added to the subscription list. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a0901699375c972b807ba5255773f017f}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-thread\-\_\-cnt@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-thread\-\_\-cnt}}

Producer\-: Set partitioner callback in provided topic conf object.

The partitioner may be called in any thread at any time, it may be called multiple times for the same message/key.

Partitioner function constraints\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item M\-U\-S\-T N\-O\-T call any rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-$\ast$() functions except\-: \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad24c6cc7f37271e292f8105c64d77758}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-available()}
\item M\-U\-S\-T N\-O\-T block or execute for prolonged periods of time.
\item M\-U\-S\-T return a value between 0 and partition\-\_\-cnt-\/1, or the special R\-D\-\_\-\-K\-A\-F\-K\-A\-\_\-\-P\-A\-R\-T\-I\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-U\-A value if partitioning could not be performed. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-new@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-new}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-conf\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{conf}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}


Creates a new topic handle for topic named {\ttfamily topic}. 

{\ttfamily conf} is an optional configuration for the topic created with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a1a7032f87e7d868b80e38d0fd0ad119e}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-conf\-\_\-new()}} that will be used instead of the default topic configuration. The {\ttfamily conf} object is freed by this function and must not be used or destroyed by the application sub-\/sequently. See {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac91b47f7733b324bf4159427e90ccd01}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-conf\-\_\-set()}} et.\-al for more information.

Topic handles are refcounted internally and calling \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-new()} again with the same topic name will return the previous topic handle without updating the original handle's configuration. Applications must eventually call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a91f46cd29d4f9abacd3ee3633c01d8ff}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-destroy()} for each succesfull call to \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-new()} to clear up resources.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the new topic handle or N\-U\-L\-L on error (use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a99c7d1faaa534befeedf23b55a88a40f}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-errno2err()} to convert system {\ttfamily errno} to an rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-resp\-\_\-err\-\_\-t error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a91f46cd29d4f9abacd3ee3633c01d8ff}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-destroy()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad24c6cc7f37271e292f8105c64d77758}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-available@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-available}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-available@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-available}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rkt, }
\item[{int32\-\_\-t}]{partition}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_ad24c6cc7f37271e292f8105c64d77758}
Check if partition is available (has a leader broker).

Returns 1 if the partition is available, else 0.

A newly allocated Topic+\-Partition list.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a0c0ab2640e5e96113ce108ab78f475d0}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-list\-\_\-destroy()} to free all resources in use by a list and the list itself. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a123ce30e08b31d4ff0fcf6ebe876173d}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-topic\-\_\-partition\-\_\-list\-\_\-add()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa90f2c92a382dbd0a090d40caa73356d}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{timeout\-\_\-ms}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_aa90f2c92a382dbd0a090d40caa73356d}
Wait for all rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t objects to be destroyed. Returns 0 if all kafka objects are now destroyed, or -\/1 if the timeout was reached. Since {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-destroy()}} is an asynch operation the {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa90f2c92a382dbd0a090d40caa73356d}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-wait\-\_\-destroyed()}} function can be used for applications where a clean shutdown is required. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a111628df6c84716c4b550f8509ac6a6d}{\index{rdkafka.\-h@{rdkafka.\-h}!rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-yield@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-yield}}
\index{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-yield@{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-yield}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-yield}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}R\-D\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-yield (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-t $\ast$}]{rk}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{rdkafka_8h_a111628df6c84716c4b550f8509ac6a6d}
Cancels the current callback dispatcher (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-consume\-\_\-callback()}, etc).

A callback may use this to force an immediate return to the calling code (caller of e.\-g. \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\-\_\-kafka\-\_\-poll()}) without processing any further events.

N\-O\-T\-E\-: This function M\-U\-S\-T O\-N\-L\-Y be called from within a librdkafka callback.
